< text>
What an absolutley great place for a bite to eat! All the produce is local/organic, all their meats and fish are grass fed, cage free, or wild caught- not to mention every single thing they plate for you is made in-house and from scratch.

The portions are very generous, and the great quality ingredients means I can leave pretty full without feeling the lethargy that comes with lower quality ingredients. Yes it's not the cheapest, (i.e. $14.00 for a salad is pretty standard), but you cant beat the quality/quantity and can share servings comfortably.

Ordered a chicken cobb salad, $14.55 after tax. I forgot to take a picture, but their website photos are fairly accurate representation, of what you should expect. Great service, great environment, great everything.

Composition: "UP lettuce blend, grilled free range chicken, organic tomatoes, turkey bacon, avocado, organic egg, blue cheese, organic sprouts - buttermilk dill dressing." (Also comes with bread).

5/5 would recommend, the dressing is amazing! Even had some left over to enjoy.<//text>

<review>This is currently one of my favorite restaurants.  I can eat anything of the menu knowing that it will be fresh and that it will taste really good.

Their plates always look vibrant and that's thanks to the variety in their menu.
The restaurant itself looks very modern and their outdoor seating is always clean and at room temperature, as they have heaters outside running when its cold.

Their service it's unmatched, always friendly and courteous, and if there is anything wrong with your order or food, they are there to make it right.

Their juice bar "Urban Replenishers" is a really great option for those looking to drink healthier things. The green super food is one of their best sellers since they make them all from scratch. I've tried all of them and they are all equally good, it really depends on what your mood is, I found that I can always drink the cantaloupe/mango and also the green tea, those are my two favs.

If they had a rewards program, it would be amazing, I know I would take advantage of it.

They also sell alcohol. But I'm not a big drinker.

Bring your family, friends or even coworkers. This is a really great place to eat.

Tip: if you order the chimichurri steak, have the chimichurri sauce on the side and not on the top, if they put it on the top... by the time you sit at your table your steak will be cold, their chimichurri sauce its served very cold.</review>< rating>

I ordered the antioxidant salad which was really good. I decided to add the baked Salmon thinking that it was wild caught but when it came I noticed it was very pale in color. That's when I asked and I learned they use sustainable Salmon, which basically means farmed. When you do the research on farmed Salmon, you  learn the negatives about it. I am very surprised they don't use wild caught, I assume it's the higher cost which would dip into their profit. Hip and healthy choice for salads and sandwiches. They have large portions and fresh entrees. Aside from salads and sandwiches, they offer soups, roasted veggies, pasta, flatbreads, desserts and other lunch/dinner platters. I recommend the chicken Cobb salad, any of the roasted veggies, hummingbird cake and cheesecake. If you‚Äôre thirsty, sample one of their homemade ‚Äúreplenishers,‚Äù kombucha, wine or beer. They also offer organic and vegetarian/vegan options. Be aware that the salad line can get very long during rush hours so plan your time accordingly. There is indoor and outdoor patio seating with water misters for those hot California days. This has become a regular spot for my friends and I, we never get sick of it! We will be back again soon!< /review>
